## v3.0.82 - 2026-01-05 06:15 HKT
**ğŸ”¬ Dual-Track Intelligent Prediction System**

### Major Features
- âœ… **Dual-Track Prediction System**: Parallel production and experimental predictions
  - Production Track: Validated weights (w_AI=0.00)
  - Experimental Track: Testing AI factor (w_AI=0.10)
- âœ… **Automatic Validation**: Real-time comparison when actual data arrives
- âœ… **Intelligent Weight Optimization**: Statistical analysis and automatic updates
  - Paired t-test for significance testing
  - Minimum 30 samples required
  - Evidence-based weight adjustments
- âœ… **Adaptive Learning**: System automatically improves based on real-world performance

### Backend
- âœ… `modules/dual-track-predictor.js`: Core dual-track engine
- âœ… `modules/pragmatic-bayesian.js`: Enhanced with dual-track support
- âœ… `python/optimize_bayesian_weights_adaptive.py`: Automatic weight optimizer
- âœ… `migrations/002_dual_track_predictions.sql`: Database schema
- âœ… API Endpoints:
  - `GET /api/dual-track/summary`: Get today's predictions + stats
  - `GET /api/dual-track/history`: Validation history for charts
  - `POST /api/dual-track/validate`: Validate predictions
  - `POST /api/dual-track/optimize`: Trigger optimization

### Frontend
- âœ… `public/dual-track.html`: Real-time dual-track dashboard
  - Live prediction comparison
  - Validation metrics display
  - Historical accuracy chart
  - System recommendations

### Database
- âœ… Extended `daily_predictions` table:
  - `prediction_production`, `prediction_experimental`
  - `production_error`, `experimental_error`
  - `better_model`, `validation_date`
- âœ… New `weight_optimization_history` table
- âœ… New `ai_factor_validation` table
- âœ… Materialized view: `validation_stats_summary`

### Documentation
- âœ… `docs/DUAL_TRACK_SYSTEM.md`: Complete system documentation
- âœ… Architecture diagrams and flow charts
- âœ… Decision criteria and examples

### AI Adaptability
- âœ… System can now automatically adapt to new AI findings
- âœ… GPT-5 or future AI updates will be validated automatically
- âœ… No manual intervention needed for AI model improvements
- âœ… Evidence-based weight updates ensure safety and reliability

**Impact**: System is now fully adaptive and will continuously improve its AI factor integration based on real-world validation data. User can see both predictions in real-time and system automatically optimizes weights when experimental track proves superior.

```javascript
    WHERE target_date = $1 
    AND prediction_time > NOW() - INTERVAL '25 minutes'
    LIMIT 1
`, [targetDate]);

    return null; // è·³éæ’å…¥
}
```

#### 2. æ–°å¢æ¸…ç† API

- è‡ªå‹•æ ¹æ“šå¯é åº¦èª¿æ•´å„ä¾†æºæ¬Šé‡

- å¯å¾æ­·å²æ•¸æ“šå­¸ç¿’æœ€å„ªå¯é åº¦

**å…¬å¼**ï¼š
```

```

**é è¨­å¯é åº¦**ï¼š
- XGBoost: 0.90 (é«˜å¯é )
- AI: 0.60 (ä¸­ç­‰å¯é ï¼Œæ–°å› ç´ )

**æœ€çµ‚é¸æ“‡**ï¼šåŠ æ¬Šçµ„åˆæ‰€æœ‰æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œæ¬Šé‡å¯å¾æ­·å²æº–ç¢ºåº¦å­¸ç¿’ã€‚
